		function topIdCheck(checkEl){
		    var objId = checkEl.id;
		    var checkObj = document.getElementById(objId);
		    var checkImgURI = checkObj.src;
		
		    if(checkImgURI.indexOf("checkBox_check.gif") == -1 ) {
		        checkObj.src = "images/common/checkBox_check.gif";
		        eval(objId+"Val = 'checked'");
		    }else {
		        checkObj.src ="images/common/checkBox.gif";
		        eval(objId+"Val = 'unchecked'");
		    }
		}


        var saveChkVal = 'unchecked';
        
        function login(){
            var userId = trim(document.loginForm.userId.value);
            var password = trim(document.loginForm.password.value); 
            var msg = "";
            if(userId.length == 0){
                msg +="아이디를 입력하세요.\n";
            }
            if(password.length == 0 &amp;&amp; msg.length == 0){
                msg +="비밀번호를 입력하세요.";
            }
            
            if(msg.length &gt; 0){
                alert(msg);
            }else{
            	var saveChkImg = document.getElementById("saveChk");
		    	if(saveChkImg.src.indexOf('_check') &gt; 0){
		    		document.loginForm.saveChkYN.value = "Y";
		    	}
                document.loginForm.submit();
            }
        }
        
        function formsubmit(evt){
            var evt = window.event || evt;
            var evCode = ( window.netscape ) ? evt.which : evt.keyCode ;
            if(evCode == 13)
                login();
        }
        
        function setCookieId(){
            if(getCookie('betman.userId') != null &amp;&amp; getCookie('betman.userId') !='null'){
                document.loginForm.userId.value = getCookie('betman.userId');
                outerLoginFocus(document.getElementById('input_id'));
                document.getElementById("saveChk").src = "images/common/checkBox_check.gif";
                saveChkVal = 'checked';
            }
        }
        
        setCookieId();

<link href="css/navi.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"/>
<script type="text/javascript">

    	var menuCode = "MN010400";
    	var naviMenuId;
    	var naviMenuIdSub;
    	try{
			naviMenuId = Number(menuCode.substring(2, 4)) - 1;
   			naviMenuIdSub = Number(menuCode.substring(4, 6)) - 1;
		}catch(e){
			naviMenuId = -1;
			naviMenuIdSub = -1;
		}finally{
			if(naviMenuId &gt; 3){
				naviMenuId = -1;
				naviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
		}
		

    	var overNaviMenuId = naviMenuId;
    	var overNaviMenuIdSub = naviMenuIdSub;
    	var isTimer = false;
    	var naviTimer;
    	
    	$(function(){

			if(naviMenuId &gt; -1 &amp;&amp; naviMenuIdSub &gt; -1){
				if(overNaviMenuId == naviMenuId){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + naviMenuId).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (naviMenuId + 1) + " selected";
				}
				
				document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).getElementsByTagName("li")[naviMenuIdSub].className = "item02 selected";
			}
		});
		
		function topNaviController1(id, animated){

			if(animated){
				if(id != overNaviMenuId){
					if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
						document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
						document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);
					}
					
					document.getElementById("ncg" + id).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + id).className = "depth02 depth020" + (id + 1) + " selected";
					
					overNaviMenuId = id;
					overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
				}
			}else{
				if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);

				}
				overNaviMenuId = -1;
				overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
    	}
    	
    	function defNaviTop(){
    		if(naviMenuId != overNaviMenuId){
				if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);
				}
				if(naviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + naviMenuId).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (naviMenuId + 1) + " selected";
				}
				overNaviMenuId = naviMenuId;
				overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
    	}
    	
    	function cancelHide(){
			clearTimeout(naviTimer);
			isTimer = false;
		}
    	
    	function hideTop(){
    		if(!isTimer){
    			isTimer = true;
    			naviTimer = setTimeout("defNaviTop()", 500);
    		}
    	}
		
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	var menuCodeLeft = "MN010400";

	$(function(){
		
		var l1 = menuCodeLeft.substring(2, 4);
		var l2 = menuCodeLeft.substring(4, 6);
		var l3 = menuCodeLeft.substring(6, 8);

		if(l2 != "00")
			document.getElementById("lui"+l2).className = "item02 selected";
		
		if(l3 != "00"){
			try{
				document.getElementById("lui"+l2+l3).className = "item03 selected";
			}catch(e){
			}finally{
			}
		}
		
		
		if( l1 == "05" &amp;&amp; l2 == "10" ){
			// 건토 즐토 일때 특정 배너 노출 처리
			document.getElementById("selfbetball").style.display = "";
		}
		
	});

<script type="text/javascript">
&lt;!--//

	


	function goPrevRound(){
		var gamePrevRound = '180067';
		if(gamePrevRound == "0"){
			alert('이전회차가 존재하지 않습니다.');
		}else{
			var actionUrl = "./winningResultProto.so?";
			var gameId = "method=detail&amp;gameId=G101&amp;";
			var gameRound = "gameRound="+gamePrevRound;
			window.location = actionUrl + gameId + gameRound;
		}
	}

function goNextRound(){
	var gameNextRound = '180069';
	
	if(gameNextRound == "0"){
		alert('다음회차가 존재하지 않습니다.');
	}else{
		var actionUrl = "./winningResultProto.so?";
		var gameId = "method=detail&amp;gameId=G101&amp;";
		var gameRound = "gameRound="+gameNextRound;
		window.location = actionUrl + gameId + gameRound;
	}
}

//--&gt;
</script>

		var sortTable = new SortTableClass("tblSort",true,'img','images/button/bts_down.gif','images/button/bts_downon.gif','images/button/bts_upon.gif');
        function formatUserDefinedImg(sValue){
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('soccer') != -1 ) return 1;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('baseball') != -1 ) return 2;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('basketball') != -1 ) return 3;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('volleyball') != -1 ) return 4;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('golf') != -1 ) return 5;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('ssireum') != -1 ) return 6;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('all') != -1 ) return 1;			// 게임유형 정렬 추가 140206
			if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('handicap') != -1 ) return 2;
			if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('uo') != -1 ) return 3;     
			if(sValue.indexOf('홀짝') != -1 ) return 4;         
            if(sValue =="") return 7;
            
        }
		</script>

		function topIdCheck(checkEl){
		    var objId = checkEl.id;
		    var checkObj = document.getElementById(objId);
		    var checkImgURI = checkObj.src;
		
		    if(checkImgURI.indexOf("checkBox_check.gif") == -1 ) {
		        checkObj.src = "images/common/checkBox_check.gif";
		        eval(objId+"Val = 'checked'");
		    }else {
		        checkObj.src ="images/common/checkBox.gif";
		        eval(objId+"Val = 'unchecked'");
		    }
		}


        var saveChkVal = 'unchecked';
        
        function login(){
            var userId = trim(document.loginForm.userId.value);
            var password = trim(document.loginForm.password.value); 
            var msg = "";
            if(userId.length == 0){
                msg +="아이디를 입력하세요.\n";
            }
            if(password.length == 0 &amp;&amp; msg.length == 0){
                msg +="비밀번호를 입력하세요.";
            }
            
            if(msg.length &gt; 0){
                alert(msg);
            }else{
            	var saveChkImg = document.getElementById("saveChk");
		    	if(saveChkImg.src.indexOf('_check') &gt; 0){
		    		document.loginForm.saveChkYN.value = "Y";
		    	}
                document.loginForm.submit();
            }
        }
        
        function formsubmit(evt){
            var evt = window.event || evt;
            var evCode = ( window.netscape ) ? evt.which : evt.keyCode ;
            if(evCode == 13)
                login();
        }
        
        function setCookieId(){
            if(getCookie('betman.userId') != null &amp;&amp; getCookie('betman.userId') !='null'){
                document.loginForm.userId.value = getCookie('betman.userId');
                outerLoginFocus(document.getElementById('input_id'));
                document.getElementById("saveChk").src = "images/common/checkBox_check.gif";
                saveChkVal = 'checked';
            }
        }
        
        setCookieId();

    //--&gt;
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    	var menuCode = "MN010400";
    	var naviMenuId;
    	var naviMenuIdSub;
    	try{
			naviMenuId = Number(menuCode.substring(2, 4)) - 1;
   			naviMenuIdSub = Number(menuCode.substring(4, 6)) - 1;
		}catch(e){
			naviMenuId = -1;
			naviMenuIdSub = -1;
		}finally{
			if(naviMenuId &gt; 3){
				naviMenuId = -1;
				naviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
		}
		

    	var overNaviMenuId = naviMenuId;
    	var overNaviMenuIdSub = naviMenuIdSub;
    	var isTimer = false;
    	var naviTimer;
    	
    	$(function(){

			if(naviMenuId &gt; -1 &amp;&amp; naviMenuIdSub &gt; -1){
				if(overNaviMenuId == naviMenuId){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + naviMenuId).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (naviMenuId + 1) + " selected";
				}
				
				document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).getElementsByTagName("li")[naviMenuIdSub].className = "item02 selected";
			}
		});
		
		function topNaviController1(id, animated){

			if(animated){
				if(id != overNaviMenuId){
					if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
						document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
						document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);
					}
					
					document.getElementById("ncg" + id).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + id).className = "depth02 depth020" + (id + 1) + " selected";
					
					overNaviMenuId = id;
					overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
				}
			}else{
				if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);

				}
				overNaviMenuId = -1;
				overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
    	}
    	
    	function defNaviTop(){
    		if(naviMenuId != overNaviMenuId){
				if(overNaviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + overNaviMenuId).className = "item01";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + overNaviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (overNaviMenuId + 1);
				}
				if(naviMenuId &gt; -1){
					document.getElementById("ncg" + naviMenuId).className = "item01 selected";
					document.getElementById("ncs" + naviMenuId).className = "depth02 depth020" + (naviMenuId + 1) + " selected";
				}
				overNaviMenuId = naviMenuId;
				overNaviMenuIdSub = -1;
			}
    	}
    	
    	function cancelHide(){
			clearTimeout(naviTimer);
			isTimer = false;
		}
    	
    	function hideTop(){
    		if(!isTimer){
    			isTimer = true;
    			naviTimer = setTimeout("defNaviTop()", 500);
    		}
    	}
		
    </script>

		var sortTable = new SortTableClass("tblSort",true,'img','images/button/bts_down.gif','images/button/bts_downon.gif','images/button/bts_upon.gif');
        function formatUserDefinedImg(sValue){
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('soccer') != -1 ) return 1;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('baseball') != -1 ) return 2;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('basketball') != -1 ) return 3;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('volleyball') != -1 ) return 4;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('golf') != -1 ) return 5;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('ssireum') != -1 ) return 6;
            if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('all') != -1 ) return 1;			// 게임유형 정렬 추가 140206
			if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('handicap') != -1 ) return 2;
			if(sValue.toLowerCase().lastIndexOf('uo') != -1 ) return 3;     
			if(sValue.indexOf('홀짝') != -1 ) return 4;         
            if(sValue =="") return 7;
            
        }
		</script>
